if ('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) {\n      const SR = window.webkitSpeechRecognition\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR()\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true\n      \n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = async (e) => {\n        let final = ''\n        for (let i = e.resultIndex; i < e.results.length; i++) {\n          if (e.results[i].isFinal) final += e.results[i][0].transcript\n        }\n        setTranscript(final || 'Listening...')\n        if (final) {\n          const res = await sendVoice(final,     const lower = text.toLowerCase()\n      if (lower.includes('dashboard')) navigate('/dashboard')\n      else if (lower.includes('properties')) navigate('/properties')\n      else if (lower.includes('home')) navigate('/')\n    }\n  }\n  \n  const speak = (text) => {\n    if (window.speechSynthesis) {\n      window.speechSynthesis.cancel()\n      window.speechSynthesis.speak(new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text))\n    }\n  }\n  \n  const toggle = () => {\n    if (isListening) {\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop()\n      setIsListening(false)\n    } else {\n      recognitionRef.current?.start()\n      setIsListening(true)\n      setTranscript('Listening...')\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return (\n    <div className=\"agentic-bar\">\n      <button className={`mic-btn ${isListening ? '\ud83d\udd34' : '\ud83c\udfa4'}\n      </button>\n      <div className=\"bar-content\">\n        <div className=\"bar-header\">\n          <span className=\"title\">\ud83e\udd16 Mr. V</span>\n          <select value={userType} onChange={e => setUserType(e.target.value)}>\n            <option value=\"boss\">\ud83d\udc64 Boss</option>\n            <option value=\"dev_team\">\ud83d\udc65 Dev</option>\n            <option value=\"vendor\">\ud83c\udfea Vendor</option>\n            <option value=\"visitor\">\ud83d\udc41\ufe0f Visitor</option>\n          </select>\n          <span className={`status ${isConnected ? \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udd17 Creating AgenticContext...\"\n\ncat > \"$VV_HOME/frontend/src/context/AgenticContext.jsx\" << 'CTXEOF'\nimport React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'\nimport { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom'\n\nconst AgenticContext = createContext(null)\nconst API = 'http://localhost:1117/api'\n\nexport const AgenticProvider = ({ children }) => {\n  const navigate = useNavigate()\n  const location = useLocation()\n  const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState(null)\n  const [userType, setUserType] = useState('visitor')\n  const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState(false)\n  const [navStack, setNavStack] = useState([])\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetch(`${API}/session/start`, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify({ user_type: userType })\n    }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {\n      if (d.session_id) { setSessionId(d.session_id); setIsConnected(true) }\n    }).catch(() => {})\n  }, [])\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    setNavStack(p => [...p, { route: location.pathname, title: document.title }])\n    if (sessionId) {\n      fetch(`${API}/navigation/push`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId, page_route: location.pathname })\n      }).catch(() => {})\n    }\n  }, [location.pathname, sessionId])\n  \n  const sendVoice = useCallback(async (text, page) => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${API}/ledger/log`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ user_type: userType, session_id: sessionId, raw_transcript: text, page_route: page })\n      })\n      return res.json()\n    } catch { return null }\n  }, [sessionId, userType])\n  \n  const goBack = useCallback(async () => {\n    if (navStack.length > 1) {\n      try {\n        const res = await fetch(`${API}/navigation/back`, {\n          method: 'POST',\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n          body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId })\n        })\n        const d = await res.json()\n        if (d.success && d.page) { setNavStack(p => p.slice(0, -1)); navigate(d.page.page_route) }\n      } catch { navigate(-1) }\n    }\n  }, [sessionId, navStack, navigate])\n  \n  const goHome = useCallback(() => { setNavStack([]); navigate('/') }, [navigate])\n  \n  return (\n    <AgenticContext.Provider value={{ sessionId, userType, setUserType, isConnected, navStack, sendVoice, goBack, goHome }}>\n      {children}\n    </AgenticContext.Provider>\n  )\n}\n\nexport const useAgentic = () => useContext(AgenticContext)\nCTXEOF\n\necho \"\u2705 Context flask_cors import CORS\nimport numpy as np\nimport hashlib\nimport os\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\nCORS(app)\n\ndef pseudo_embedding(text, dim=1536):\n    h = hashlib.sha512(text.encode()).hexdigest()\n    emb = [(int(h[i%64*2:i%64*2+2], 16)/255)*2-1 for i in range(dim)]\n    mag = np.sqrt(sum(v**2 for v in emb))\n    return [v/mag for v in emb]\n\n@app.route('/health')\ndef health():\n    return   { text: res.analysis.emotion, type: 'emotion' },\\n              { text: res.analysis.intent, type: 'intent' }\\n            ])\\n            handleIntent(res.analysis.intent, final)\\n          }\\n          if (res?.tts_response?.text) speak(res.tts_response.text)\\n        }\\n      }\\n      \\n      recognitionRef.current.onend = () => { if (isListening) recognitionRef.current.start() }\\n    }\\n  }, [isListening])\\n  \\n  const handleIntent = (intent, text) => {\\n    if (intent === 'system_back') goBack()\\n    else if (intent === 'system_close') goHome()\\n    else if (intent === 'navigation') {\\n      const lower = text.toLowerCase()\\n      if (lower.includes('dashboard')) navigate('/dashboard')\\n      else if (lower.includes('properties')) navigate('/properties')\\n      else if (lower.includes('home')) navigate('/')\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  const speak = (text) => {\\n    if (window.speechSynthesis) {\\n      window.speechSynthesis.cancel()\\n      window.speechSynthesis.speak(new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text))\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  const toggle = () => {\\n    if (isListening) {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop()\\n      setIsListening(false)\\n    } else {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.start()\\n      setIsListening(true)\\n      setTranscript('Listening...')\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <div '\\ud83d\\udd34' : '\\ud83c\\udfa4'}\\n      </button>\\n      <div className=\\\"bar-content\\\">\\n        <div className=\\\"bar-header\\\">\\n          <span className=\\\"title\\\">\\ud83e\\udd16 Mr. V</span>\\n          <select value={userType} onChange={e => setUserType(e.target.value)}>\\n            <option value=\\\"boss\\\">\\ud83d\\udc64 Boss</option>\\n            <option value=\\\"dev_team\\\">\\ud83d\\udc65 Dev</option>\\n            <option value=\\\"vendor\\\">\\ud83c\\udfea Vendor</option>\\n            <option value=\\\"visitor\\\">\\ud83d\\udc41\\ufe0f Visitor</option>\\n          </select>\\n          <span className={`status ${isConnected ? \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udd17 Creating AgenticContext...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VV_HOME/frontend/src/context/AgenticContext.jsx\\\" << 'CTXEOF'\\nimport React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'\\nimport { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom'\\n\\nconst AgenticContext = createContext(null)\\nconst API = 'http://localhost:1117/api'\\n\\nexport const AgenticProvider = ({ children }) => {\\n  const navigate = useNavigate()\\n  const location = useLocation()\\n  const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState(null)\\n  const [userType, setUserType] = useState('visitor')\\n  const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState(false)\\n  const [navStack, setNavStack] = useState([])\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    fetch(`${API}/session/start`, {\\n      method: 'POST',\\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n      body: JSON.stringify({ user_type: userType })\\n    }).then(r => r.json()).then(d => {\\n      if (d.session_id) { setSessionId(d.session_id); setIsConnected(true) }\\n    }).catch(() => {})\\n  }, [])\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    setNavStack(p => [...p, { route: location.pathname, title: document.title }])\\n    if (sessionId) {\\n      fetch(`${API}/navigation/push`, {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId, page_route: location.pathname })\\n      }).catch(() => {})\\n    }\\n  }, [location.pathname, sessionId])\\n  \\n  const sendVoice = useCallback(async (text, page) => {\\n    try {\\n      const res = await fetch(`${API}/ledger/log`, {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ user_type: userType, session_id: sessionId, raw_transcript: text, page_route: page })\\n      })\\n      return res.json()\\n    } catch { return null }\\n  }, [sessionId, userType])\\n  \\n  const goBack = useCallback(async () => {\\n    if (navStack.length > 1) {\\n      try {\\n        const res = await fetch(`${API}/navigation/back`, {\\n          method: 'POST',\\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n          body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId })\\n        })\\n        const d = await res.json()\\n        if (d.success && d.page) { setNavStack(p => p.slice(0, -1)); navigate(d.page.page_route) }\\n      } catch { navigate(-1) }\\n    }\\n  }, [sessionId, navStack, navigate])\\n  \\n  const goHome = useCallback(() => { setNavStack([]); navigate('/') }, [navigate])\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <AgenticContext.Provider value={{ sessionId, userType, setUserType, isConnected, navStack, sendVoice, goBack, goHome }}>\\n Flask, request, jsonify\\nfrom flask_cors import CORS\\nimport numpy as np\\nimport hashlib\\nimport os\\n\\napp = Flask(__name__)\\nCORS(app)\\n\\ndef pseudo_embedding(text, dim=1536):\\n    h = hashlib.sha512(text.encode()).hexdigest()\\n    emb = [(int(h[i%64*2:i%64*2+2], 16)/255)*2-1 for i in range(dim)]\\n    mag = np.sqrt(sum(v**2 for v in emb))\\n    return [v/mag for v in emb]\\n\\n@app.route('/health')\\ndef health():\\n    return jsonify({'status': 'ok', 'embedder': 'pseudo'})\\n\\n@app.route('/embed', methods=['POST'])\\ndef embed():\\n    text = 1536})\\n\\n@app.route('/similarity', methods=['POST'])\\ndef similarity():\\n    t1, t2 = request.json.get('text1', ''), request.json.get('text2', '')\\n    e1, e2 = np.array(pseudo_embedding(t1)), np.array(pseudo_embedding(t2))\\n    sim = float(np.dot(e1, e2) / (np.linalg.norm(e1) * np.linalg.norm(e2)))\\n    return jsonify({'similarity': sim})\\n\\nif __name__ == '__main__':\\n e.clientY;\n        });\n        \n        function animateCursor() {\n            cursorX += (targetX - cursorX) * 0.1;\n            cursorY += (targetY - cursorY) * 0.1;\n            cursor.style.left = cursorX + 'px';\n            cursor.style.top = cursorY + 'px';\n            \n            // Flip based on direction\n            if (targetX > cursorX + 5) cursor.style.transform animateCursor();\n        \n        // Time\n        function updateTime() {\n            document.getElementById('currentTime').textContent = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n        }\n       recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n            \n            recognition.onresult = async (e) => {\n                let final = '', interim = '';\n                for (let i = e.resultIndex; i < e.results.length; i++) {\n                    if (e.results[i].isFinal) final += e.results[i][0].transcript;\n                    else interim += e.results[i][0].transcript;\n                }\n                \n                document.getElementById('transcript').textContent = interim || final || 'Listening...';\n                \n                if (final) {\n                    await function startRecording() {\n            if (!recognition) return alert('Use Chrome for voice');\n            recognition.start();\n            isRecording = true;\n
